#USS Cole Attacks
country_event = {
	id = usa.2
	title = usa.2.t
	desc = usa.2.d
	picture = GFX_uss_cole_bombing
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
	}

	# They Will be Missed
	option = {
		name = usa.2.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.2.o1 executed"

		news_event = { hours = 6 id = usa_news.18 }
		add_named_threat = { threat = 0.5 name = usa.2.t }

		# Hate on SUD
		if = { limit = { country_exists = SUD }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = SUD modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SUD modifier = recent_actions_negative }
		}
		else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
					NOT = { tag = SAU }
					NOT = { tag = UAE }
					NOT = { tag = OMA }
					NOT = { tag = QAT }
					NOT = { tag = BHR }
					NOT = { tag = KUW }
					NOT = { tag = JOR }
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			}
		}
		USA_congress_small_opposition = yes
		set_country_flag = usa_uss_cole_attack

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

	#Demand Sudan Repay!
	option = {
		name = usa.2.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.2.o2 executed"

		news_event = { hours = 6 id = usa_news.18 }
		navy_experience = 5
		add_named_threat = { threat = 0.5 name = usa.2.t }

		#  Demand Repayment!
		if = { limit = { country_exists = SUD }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = SUD modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SUD modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			SUD = { country_event = { id = usa.2000 days = 7 random_hours = 2 } }
		}
		else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
					NOT = { tag = SAU }
					NOT = { tag = UAE }
					NOT = { tag = OMA }
					NOT = { tag = QAT }
					NOT = { tag = BHR }
					NOT = { tag = KUW }
					NOT = { tag = JOR }
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
				country_event = { id = usa.2000 days = 7 random_hours = 2 }
			}
		}
		USA_congress_small_opposition = yes
		set_country_flag = usa_uss_cole_attack

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 0.25
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0.25
				has_government = nationalist
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
	}
}

#Sudan - America Demands Repayment for the USS Cole Bombing
country_event = {
	id = usa.2000
	title = usa.2000.t
	desc = usa.2000.d
	picture = GFX_uss_cole_bombing
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		USA = { has_country_flag = usa_uss_cole_attack }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
	}

	option = { #Accept
		name = usa.2000.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.2000.o1 executed"
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.25 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			USA = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 0.25 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
		}

		#Response sent to America
		USA = { country_event = { id = usa.2001 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse
		name = usa.2000.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.2000.o2 executed"
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.02 }
		recalculate_party = yes

		USA = { country_event = { id = usa.2002 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Microsoft acquires Visio
country_event = {
	id = usa.4
	title = usa.4.t
	desc = usa.4.d
	picture = GFX_stock_market
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_government = communism }
			NOT = { has_government = nationalist }
			NOT = {	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } }
			NOT = {	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } }
			NOT = {	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } }
			NOT = {	is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } }
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
	}

	#Allow the Acqusition
	option = {
		name = usa.4.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.4.o1 executed"
		add_stability = -0.04
		811 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = USA_allowed_microsoft_merger
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_economic_regulation = -4 }
		USA_modify_economic_regulation = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_wall_street = 3 }
		USA_modify_strength_of_wall_street = yes

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 3 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes

		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = usa.5 days = 25 random_hours = 10 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = USA_REPUBLICAN_PATH
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

	#Stop the Merger!
	option = {
		name = usa.4.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.4.o2 executed"
		add_stability = 0.02
		811 = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2 }
		set_country_flag = USA_stopped_microsoft_merger
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_economic_regulation = 4 }
		USA_modify_economic_regulation = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_wall_street = -2 }
		USA_modify_strength_of_wall_street = yes

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes

		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = usa.5 days = 25 random_hours = 10 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = USA_REFORMED_REPUBLIC_PATH
				add = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

#America Online merges with Time Warner
country_event = {
	id = usa.5
	title = usa.5.t
	desc = usa.5.d
	picture = GFX_stock_market
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
			has_government = nationalist
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
			is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 }
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = USA_stopped_microsoft_merger
			has_country_flag = USA_allowed_microsoft_merger
		}
		date > 2000.2.1
		date < 2016.01.01
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Excellent!
	option = {
		name = usa.5.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.5.o1 executed"
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_economic_regulation = -4 }
		USA_modify_economic_regulation = yes

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 2 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1.5
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = USA_REPUBLICAN_PATH
				add = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 0.75
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.10
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0.50
				has_country_flag = USA_allowed_microsoft_merger
			}
		}
	}

	#This is Illegal!
	option = {
		name = usa.5.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.5.o2 executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { modify_economic_regulation = 5 }
		USA_modify_economic_regulation = yes

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -3 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0.50
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = USA_REFORMED_REPUBLIC_PATH
				add = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 0.30
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.50
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0.75
				has_country_flag = USA_stopped_microsoft_merger
			}
		}
	}
}

#Elian Gonzalez Affair
country_event = {
	id = usa.7
	title = usa.7.t
	desc = usa.7.d
	picture = GFX_elian_gonzalez
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_government = communism }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
		CUB = {
			has_government = communism
			exists = yes
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {	#Send the boy back
		name = usa.7.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.7.o1 executed"
		add_political_power = 50
		CUB = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_positive }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -3 }
		change_communist_cadres_opinion = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				80 = {
					country_event = { id = usa.22 days = 112 random_hours = 15 }
				}
				20 = {
					country_event = { id = usa.23 days = 112 random_hours = 15 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa.7.o1_tt

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } #Republican
				add = 0.25
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Keep him here
		name = usa.7.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.7.o2 executed"
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = 0.03
		CUB = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_communist_cadres_opinion = yes

		add_named_threat = { threat = 2.5 name = usa.7.t }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
	}
}

#Greeneville sinks Ehime-Maru
country_event = {
	id = usa.8
	title = usa.8.t
	desc = usa.8.d
	picture = GFX_ehimemaru
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
	}

	option = {	#Apologize
		name = usa.8.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.8.o1 executed"
		add_stability = -0.01
		set_temp_variable = { arg_popularity = -0.01 }
		add_ruling_outlook_popularity = yes
		JAP = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_positive }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 0.25
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0.10
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#It's their fault
		name = usa.8.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.8.o2 executed"
		add_named_threat = { threat = 0.5 name = usa.8.t }
		set_temp_variable = { arg_popularity = -0.02 }
		add_ruling_outlook_popularity = yes
		JAP = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_negative }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				has_government = communism
				has_government = nationalist
				add = 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				add = 0.25
			}
		}
	}
}

#2000 Phillips Explosion
country_event = {
	id = usa.12
	title = usa.12.t
	desc = usa.12.d
	picture = GFX_burning_oil_refinery
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_full_control_of_state = 800	#Texas
		date > 2000.03.20
		date < 2000.04.1
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
	}

	option = { #Accidents Happen
		name = usa.12.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.12.o1 executed"
		add_stability = -0.04
		USA_congress_medium_opposition = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
				}
				add = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Launch a Complete Investigation
		name = usa.12.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.12.o2 executed"
		add_political_power = -75
		add_stability = -0.02
		USA_congress_small_opposition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.25 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_intelligence_community_opinion = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
		change_fossil_fuel_industry_opinion = yes
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
				}
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } #Conservatism
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 } #Libertarian
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } #RWP
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 }
				}
				add = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

##Main Dispatch Event##
country_event = {
	id = usa.1000
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
	}
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa.1000 executed"
		random_list = {
			#Political Establishment Reinforced
			60 = {
				modifier = {
					congress_low_support_trigger = yes
					factor = 1.25
				}
				modifier = {
					has_idea = political_establishment
					factor = 5
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.21 days = 21 random_hours = 5 }
			}
			#Third Party Gains
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					NOT = { congress_low_support_trigger = yes }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				modifier = {
					has_stability > 0.40
					factor = 1.5
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.18 days = 20 random_hours = 5 }
			}
			#Rise of Leftism
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					has_stability > 0.40
					factor = 1.5
				}
				modifier = {
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^2 > 0.10 }
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^3 > 0.10 }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				modifier = {
					NOT = { congress_low_support_trigger = yes }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.17 days = 20 random_hours = 5 }
			}
			#Rise of Traditionalism
			8 = {
				modifier = {
					has_stability > 0.40
					factor = 1.5
				}
				modifier = {
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^1 > 0.10 }
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^14 > 0.10 }
					check_variable = { party_pop_array^20 > 0.10 }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				modifier = {
					NOT = { congress_low_support_trigger = yes }
					factor = 1.25
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.19 days = 20 random_hours = 5 }
			}
			#Anti-Globalization Protests
			7 = {
				modifier = {
					has_government = nationalist
					factor = 1.25
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.20 days = 20 random_hours = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 3 }

		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		}

				has_idea = NATO_member
			}
			NATO_leave = yes
		}

			USA = { country_event = diplomatic_response.1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = seeks_american_alliance
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				add = -100
			}
		}
	}

		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				add = 50
			}
		}
	}

#Microsoft allowed to expand further
country_event = {
	id = usa.33
	title = usa.33.t
	desc = usa.33.d
	picture = GFX_court
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
	}

	#Increased Economic Prosperity
	option = {
		name = usa.33.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.33.o1 executed"
		increase_economic_growth = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				811 = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 1
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
			}
			811 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				811 = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size = 0
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 7 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes

		set_country_flag = USA_allowed_microsoft_monopoly
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = USA_death_of_gus_hall
	}
	title = usa.60.t
	desc = usa.60.d
	picture = GFX_fathers_of_communism
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_death_of_gus_hall }
		date > 2000.10.01
		date < 2001.10.31
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
	}

	option = {
		name = usa.60.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.60.o1 executed"
		add_stability = 0.02

		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}

	option = {
		name = usa.60.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.60.o2 executed"
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.01
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 3 }
		change_communist_cadres_opinion = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { gov_coalition_array = 4 }
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = communist_sympathizer
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = communism }
				country_event = { id = usa.63 days = 1000 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
}

#US Armoured Brigade in E-Europe Activated - Spawns in Warsaw
country_event = {
	id = USA_FOCUS.2
	title = USA_FOCUS.2.t
	desc = USA_FOCUS.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_american_troops
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
	}

	#Deploy - the E-Brigade
	option = {
		name = USA_FOCUS.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_FOCUS.2.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_template = "Armored Brigade"
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Armored Brigade"
					regiments = {
						armor_Bat = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						armor_Bat = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						Arm_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						Arm_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						SP_Arty_Bat = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						Arm_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						Mech_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					}

					support = {
						H_Engi_Comp = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						SP_Arty_Battery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			114 = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Armored Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 0.50"
					owner = USA
					prioritize_location = 3544
					count = 1
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_deploy_e_brigade_tt
		news_event = { id = USA_FOCUS.1 days = 1 }
	}
}

	desc = USA_FOCUS.10.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		country_exists = ISI

	}

		name = USA_FOCUS.10.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_FOCUS.10.a executed"
		ROJ = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_weapons3 amount = 2000 producer = USA }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = util_vehicle_4 amount = 100 producer = USA }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = Anti_tank_1 amount = 500 producer = USA }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = USA_ROJ_ARMED }
		}
		TUR = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = USA_TUR_ARM_KURDS }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_Armed_ROJ
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
	}

	option = { #No
		name = USA_FOCUS.10.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_FOCUS.10.b executed"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0.5
		}
	}

}

###American Economic Events###
##2000's Recession
country_event = {
	id = usa_economic_events.init
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		date > 2005.1.1
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = collapsed_nation
				has_country_flag = USA_housing_problems_detected
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 90 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var > 90 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var < 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3.5
			check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var > 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_idea = wall_street
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.10
			date > 2009.1.01
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = usa_great_financial_crisis #Global Flag for other Content Designing
		country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.1 days = 10 random_hours = 5 }
	}
}

##The Lehman Brothers Collapse!
country_event = {
	id = usa_economic_events.1
	title = usa_economic_events.1.t
	desc = usa_economic_events.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_lehmanbrothers
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = collapsed_nation
				has_country_flag = USA_housing_problems_detected
			}
		}
	}

	#Oh no, nationalize it!
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.1.a"
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -90 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		recession = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa_economic_nationalize_tt

		set_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.2 days = 40 random_hours = 30 }
			news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.1 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_government = nationalist
					has_government = communism
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				nationalist > 0.30
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	#Bailout the bank!
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.1.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.1.b"
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -60 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		recession = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa_economic_bailout_tt

		#Obama/Democrat Route to handling the crisis
		set_country_flag = usa_bailout_one
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.2 days = 40 random_hours = 30 }
			news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.1 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_government = nationalist
					has_government = communism
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 }
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 5
			}
		}
	}

	#Let it take its course
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.1.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.1.c"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		recession = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
		change_wall_street_opinion = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = usa_economic_donothing_tt

		#Begins the Libertarian/Republican Method of a Laissez Faire Approach
		set_country_flag = usa_nothing_one
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.1 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.2 days = 40 random_hours = 30 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_government = nationalist
					has_government = communism
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
				is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.2 days = 2 }
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.3 days = 40 random_hours = 30 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				add = 0.25
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = neutrality
				add = 0.25
			}
		}
	}

		NOT = {

				has_country_flag = collapsed_nation

		}
	}

		name = usa_economic_events.3.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.3.a"

		set_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.3 days = 2 }
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.4 days = 40 random_hours = 30 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
	#Allow the Merger
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.3.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.3.a"

			news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.3 days = 2 }
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.4 days = 40 random_hours = 30 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

			news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.3 days = 2 }
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.4 days = 40 random_hours = 30 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

#The Housing Market Crashes!
country_event = {
	id = usa_economic_events.5
	immediate = {
		CAN = { country_event = { id = canada.600 days = 1 } } #Canada Recession Event
	}
	title = usa_economic_events.5.t
	desc = usa_economic_events.5.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_foreclosure
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_country_flag = usa_american_recession_occured }
	}

	#So?
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.5.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.5.a"
		add_political_power = 50
		if = { #Bailout and Nationalization - Nationalization is the most unstable. It is very unpredictable
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_four
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_three
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_two
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_one
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var > 30 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 40 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		else_if = { #Bailout and Nationalization
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_four
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_three
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_two
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var > 10 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 60 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = -0.025
		}
		else_if = { #Nationalization and Noting Can Lead Here
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_one
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var < 40 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 90 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
			add_political_power = 150
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.30 days = 70 random_hours = 35 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } #conservatism
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 }
				}
				add = 0.30
			}
		}
	}

	#Assist the Families
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.5.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.5.b"
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -150 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_stability = 0.03
		if = { #Bailout and Nationalization - Nationalization is the most unstable. It is very unpredictable
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_four
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_three
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_two
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_one
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var > 30 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 40 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		else_if = { #Bailout and Nationalization
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_four
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_three
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_two
					has_country_flag = usa_bailout_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var > 10 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 60 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = -0.025
		}
		else_if = { #Nationalization and Noting Can Lead Here
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 5
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nothing_one
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_four
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_three
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_two
					has_country_flag = usa_nationalize_one
					check_variable = { USA_strength_of_wall_street_var < 40 }
					check_variable = { USA_economic_regulation_var < 90 }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
			add_political_power = 150
			add_stability = -0.05
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.30 days = 70 random_hours = 35 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 2
			}

				is_historical_focus_on = no

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] event usa_economic_events.3"

			##Military Industry Leave the USA
			5 = {
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.31 days = 100 random_hours = 35 }
			}
			##Civilian Factories Leave the USA
			30 = {
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.32 days = 100 random_hours = 35 }
			}
			##Company Collapse
			15 = {
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.33 days = 100 random_hours = 35 }
			}
			##Company Goes Bankrupt
			50 = {
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.34 days = 100 random_hours = 35 }
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
		has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
		has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
		NOT = { has_country_flag = usa_american_recession_occured }
	}

#Military Industry Leaves the USA
country_event = {
	id = usa_economic_events.31
	title = usa_economic_events.31.t
	desc = usa_economic_events.31.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_handgun
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = usa_american_recession_occured }
	}
	#Oh no
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.31.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.31.a"
		set_temp_variable = { arg_popularity = -0.02 }
		add_ruling_outlook_popularity = yes
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			remove_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			remove_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = recession
				}
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.30 days = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_idea = recession }
				}
				country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.35 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

		OR = {
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
		}
		has_idea = recession
		NOT = { has_country_flag = usa_american_recession_occured }
	}

	#Oh no
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.32.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.32.a"
		set_temp_variable = { arg_popularity = -0.02 }
		add_ruling_outlook_popularity = yes
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = usa_economic_events.30 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

#End of the American Recession
country_event = {
	id = usa_economic_events.35
	title = usa_economic_events.35.t
	desc = usa_economic_events.35.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_banking_crisis
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_global_flag = usa_great_financial_crisis
		OR = {
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = stable_growth
			has_idea = fast_growth
			has_idea = economic_boom
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = usa_american_recession_occured
			has_country_flag = USA_american_recession_over
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
		modifier = {
			factor = 25
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 20
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1000
			OR = {
				has_idea = recession
				has_idea = depression
				has_idea = stagnation
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			OR = {
				has_idea = stable_growth
				has_idea = fast_growth
				has_idea = economic_boom
			}
		}
	}
	#Glorious!
	option = {
		name = usa_economic_events.35.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event usa_economic_events.35.a"
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea }
			remove_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_light_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea }
			remove_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_medium_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea }
			remove_ideas = USA_economic_crisis_severe_idea
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_american_recession_over

		news_event = { id = usa_economic_events_news.6 days = 1 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	desc = donald_trump.8.d
	picture = GFX_trump_announcement
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Just need to wait for an asteroid...
		name = donald_trump.8.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.8.o1 executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = donald_trump.9
				days = 10
				random_hours = 4800
			}
		}
		news_event = donald_trump_news.2
		custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_wait_period_tt
	}
}

	desc = donald_trump.9.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

			country_event = {

				random_hours = 1200
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_spotted_tt
	}
}
#Asteroid in Orbit
country_event = {
	id = donald_trump.10
	title = donald_trump.10.t
	desc = donald_trump.10.d
	picture = GFX_asteroid_in_orbit
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Mining shall begin
		name = donald_trump.10.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.10.o1 executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = donald_trump.11
				days = 100
				random_hours = 2400
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_orbit_tt
		add_to_variable = { asteroid_mining_rate = 2 } #It's set here so the next event's localization isn't screwed up
		add_to_variable = { global.asteroid_mining_rate = 2 }
	}
}
#Profits from Mining Start Pouring in
country_event = {
	id = donald_trump.11
	title = donald_trump.11.t
	desc = donald_trump.11.d
	picture = GFX_asteroid_in_orbit
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Huzzah!
		name = donald_trump.11.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.11.o1 executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.002 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		capital_scope = {
			add_resource = {
				type = tungsten
				amount = 1
			}
			add_resource = {
				type = steel
				amount = 2
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.asteroid_mineral_count = 100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_mined_tt
		add_to_variable = { treasury = asteroid_mining_rate }
		custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_revenue_tt
		set_country_flag = asteroid_mining
		news_event = donald_trump_news.3
	}
}
#Profits from Asteroid Mining
country_event = {
	id = donald_trump.12
	title = donald_trump.12.t
	desc = donald_trump.12.d
	picture = GFX_asteroid_in_orbit

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Excellent!
		name = donald_trump.12.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.12.o1 executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = global.asteroid_mineral_count
					value = asteroid_mining_rate
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_mined_tt
			add_to_variable = { treasury = asteroid_mining_rate }
			subtract_from_variable = { global.asteroid_mineral_count = asteroid_mining_rate }
			custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_revenue_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_not_enough_tt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = asteroid_mining_start }
				}
				set_global_flag = asteroid_mining_start
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						num_of_factories > 40
					}
					country_event = { days = 20 id = donald_trump.13 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
#Potential for Asteroid Mining
country_event = {
	id = donald_trump.13
	title = donald_trump.13.t
	desc = donald_trump.13.d
	picture = GFX_asteroid_in_orbit
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Invest in Asteroid Mining
		name = donald_trump.13.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.13.o1 executed"
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -25 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_to_variable = { asteroid_mining_rate = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { global.asteroid_mining_rate = 1 }
		capital_scope = {
			add_resource = {
				type = steel
				amount = 1
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = asteroid_mining_opportunity_tt
		set_country_flag = asteroid_mining
		set_global_flag = asteroid_mining
	}
	option = { #Too expensive and a waste of our time!
		name = donald_trump.13.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: donald_trump.13.o2 executed"
	}
}

#Post 9/11 Reponse
country_event = {
	id = USA_events_domestic_policies.1
	title = USA_events_domestic_policies.1.t
	desc = USA_events_domestic_policies.1.d
	picture = GFX_american_troops
	major = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
	}

	option = {
		name = USA_events_domestic_policies.1.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_events_domestic_policies.1.o1 executed"
		add_stability = -0.15
		set_country_flag = USA_country_flag_arms_dealer

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_domestic_policies_tooltip
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = -0.10 }
		USA_change_domestic_political_power_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = -0.02 }
		USA_change_domestic_offensive_foreign_influence_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = 0.01 }
		USA_change_domestic_foreign_influence_defense_change = yes

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_blank_space_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_american_tax_code_tooltip
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = -0.08 }
		USA_change_tax_code_military_tax_collection_efficiency_change = yes
		USA_change_tax_code_dockyard_tax_collection_efficiency_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = 0.02 }
		USA_change_tax_code_civilian_tax_collection_efficiency_change = yes

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_blank_space_tooltip
		USA_congress_medium_opposition = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = USA_DEMOCRAT_PATH
				factor = 1000
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA_events_domestic_policies.1.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_events_domestic_policies.1.o2 executed"
		add_stability = 0.04
		add_war_support = 0.04
		set_country_flag = USA_country_flag_legal_interventionism

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_domestic_policies_tooltip
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = -0.05 }
		USA_change_domestic_political_power_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = 0.01 }
		USA_change_domestic_offensive_foreign_influence_change = yes
		USA_change_domestic_foreign_influence_defense_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = 0.01 }
		USA_change_domestic_neutrality_drift_change = yes
		USA_change_domestic_nationalist_drift_change = yes

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_blank_space_tooltip
		USA_congress_small_opposition = yes

		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = USA_events_domestic_policies.1.o3
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_events_domestic_policies.1.o3 executed"
		add_war_support = 0.10
		set_country_flag = USA_country_flag_war_on_terror

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_domestic_policies_tooltip
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = -0.06 }
		USA_change_domestic_political_power_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = 0.01 }
		USA_change_domestic_offensive_foreign_influence_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = -0.01 }
		USA_change_domestic_foreign_influence_defense_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = -0.01 }
		USA_change_domestic_communist_drift_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = 0.01 }
		USA_change_domestic_democratic_drift_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = 0.02 }
		USA_change_domestic_nationalist_drift_change = yes

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_blank_space_tooltip
		USA_congress_medium_opposition = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1

				is_historical_focus_on = yes

			}

		}
	}

# Iowa Class Event
country_event = {
	id = USA_events_domestic_policies.20
	title = {
		text = USA_events_domestic_policies.20.title1
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
				USA = {
					has_navy_size = {
						size > 1
						archetype = battleship_hull_0
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				has_navy_size = {
					size > 1
					archetype = battle_cruiser
				}
			}
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = USA_events_domestic_policies.20.title2

country_event = {

	title = USA_econ_event.11.t

	picture = GFX_stock_market
	major = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {

		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = collapsed_nation
				has_country_flag = USA_housing_problems_detected
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Sell! Sell! Sell!
		name = USA_econ_event.11.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_econ_event.11.o1 executed"

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_dynamic_modifier_department_of_the_interior_tooltip

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_blank_space_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_american_tax_code_tooltip
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = -0.03 }
		USA_change_tax_code_tax_collection_efficiency_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = -0.03 }
		USA_change_tax_code_corporate_tax_collection_efficiency_change = yes
		USA_change_tax_code_office_park_tax_collection_efficiency_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = 0.55 }
		USA_change_tax_code_interest_rate_change = yes

		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_blank_space_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_us_economic_policies_tooltip
		set_temp_variable = { temp_change = -0.500 }
		USA_change_economy_productivity_change = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = USA_the_global_financial_crisis
			days = 548
		}

		# LUIGI DO NOT TOUCH
		# Event trigger for the Eurozone Reforms
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = global.EU_member
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				random_scope_in_array = {
					array = global.EU_member
					limit = { is_ai = no }

					country_event = { id = EUevent.7 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_scope_in_array = {
					array = global.EU_member
					country_event = { id = EUevent.7 }
				}
			}
		}

		decrease_economic_growth = yes

		ingame_update_setup = yes
		767 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = offices
				level = 2
			}
		}
		769 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = offices
				level = 2
			}
		}
		770 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = offices
				level = 2
			}
		}
		772 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = offices
				level = 2
			}
		}
		773 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = offices
				level = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

				factor = 1000
			}
		}

country_event = {
	id = USA_crisis_event.1120
	title = USA_crisis_event.1120.t
	desc = USA_crisis_event.1120.d
	picture = GFX_politics_protest
	major = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TEX
	}

	option = { # Defenses
		name = USA_crisis_event.1120.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: USA_crisis_event.1120.o1 executed"

		if = {
			limit = { has_tech = infantry_weapons4 }
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_weapons2
				amount = 2000
				producer = TEX
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_tech = infantry_weapons3 }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_weapons1
				amount = 2000
				producer = TEX
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "National Guard Brigade" }
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"National Guard Brigade\" division_template = \"National Guard Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 1.5"
					owner = ROOT
					count = 10
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			division_template = {
				name = "National Guard Brigade"
				support = {
					H_Engi_Comp = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					Mot_Recce_Comp = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					combat_service_support_company = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
				regiments = {
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 3 y = 0 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					L_Inf_Bat = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				}
				priority = 0
			}
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"National Guard Brigade\" division_template = \"National Guard Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 1.5"
					owner = ROOT
					count = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				amount = 100
				Producer = USA
			}

				Producer = USA

# USS Cole News Event
news_event = {
	id = usa_news.18
	title = usa_news.18.t
	desc = usa_news.18.d
	picture = GFX_cole_attack

	major = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa_news.18.o1
		trigger = { original_tag = USA }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa_news.18.o1 executed"
	}

	option = {
		name = usa_news.18.o2
		trigger = {
			NOT = { original_tag = USA }
			NOT = { original_tag = NKO }
			NOT = { original_tag = SUD }
			NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa_news.18.o2 executed"
	}

	option = {
		name = usa_news.18.o3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = NKO
				has_war_with = USA
			}
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa_news.18.o3 executed"
	}

	option = {
		name = usa_news.18.o4
		trigger = {
			original_tag = SUD
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			USA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = SUD
					modifier = recent_actions_negative
				}
			}
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa_news.18.o4 executed"
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = usa.80
	title = usa.80.t
	desc = usa.80.d
	picture = GFX_f_plane_usa

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		NOT = { has_country_flag = collapsed_nation }
		has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
	}

	# Good Idea!
	option = {
		name = usa.80.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.80.o1 executed"
		set_country_flag = USA_started_f35_program
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_unlock_f35_decision_TT
		newline = yes
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = gdp_total }
		multiply_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.03 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		set_country_flag = USA_accepted_into_f35_program
		USA = {
			add_to_variable = { var = USA_f35_progress value = 10 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_f35_progress min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
	# Forget It
	option = {
		name = usa.80.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: usa.80.o2 executed"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Bernie Sanders" ruling_only = yes }
				add = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		set_country_flag = USA_accepted_into_f35_program
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

				annex_country = {
					target = FROM
				}

				}

			}

		}
	}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

	id = department_of_state.93
	title = department_of_state.93.t
	desc = department_of_state.93.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CSB
				}
				THIS = {
					transfer_state_to = CSB
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = RUS
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = CSB
						is_core_of = ESB
						is_core_of = KOM
						is_core_of = KAE
						is_core_of = TAT
						is_core_of = BSH
						is_core_of = DON
					}
				}
				THIS = {
					transfer_state_to = RUS
				}
			}

				}
				THIS = {

				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {

				}

country_event = {
	id = department_of_state.200
	title = department_of_state.200.t
	desc = department_of_state.200.d
	picture = GFX_USA_afghanistan_casualties
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = USA_disabled_casualty_report
		}
	}
	option = { # Okay
		name = department_of_state.200.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: department_of_state.200.a executed"
		add_manpower = -75
		newline = yes
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				add_command_power = -50
			}
			10 = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -4.54 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
			10 = {
				set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			}
			10 = {
				add_political_power = -200
			}
			10 = {
				army_experience = -25
			}
			50 = {
				# Nothing
			}
		}
		newline = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_disable_report_TT
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}
